        \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} [ \hyperlink{validate_8js_afb8e110345c45e74478894341ab6b28e}{null}, \hyperlink{validate_8js_afb8e110345c45e74478894341ab6b28e}{null}, \hyperlink{validate_8js_afb8e110345c45e74478894341ab6b28e}{null}, hsla[ 3 ] ];
    \}
    var \hyperlink{data_tables_8scroller_8min_8js_a7ddc97992591bc8a855e841ba3ee5d32}{h} = hsla[ 0 ] / 360,
        \hyperlink{validate_8js_ae059f217efaf1d50696a1214c3ce5748}{s} = hsla[ 1 ],
        \hyperlink{jquery_8data_tables_8min_8js_aae3c400cfa9afd0584b6226ac3804a40}{l} = hsla[ 2 ],
        \hyperlink{chosen_8jquery_8min_8js_a4124bc0a9335c27f086f24ba207a4912}{a} = hsla[ 3 ],
        \hyperlink{_fixed_columns_8min_8js_a53e2359402d7f3765cf1cda82ee7c11b}{q} = l <= 0.5 ? l * ( 1 + \hyperlink{validate_8js_ae059f217efaf1d50696a1214c3ce5748}{s} ) : l + \hyperlink{validate_8js_ae059f217efaf1d50696a1214c3ce5748}{s} - l * \hyperlink{validate_8js_ae059f217efaf1d50696a1214c3ce5748}{s},
        \hyperlink{media_2js_2jquery_8js_a32d2366ed9853870f0c2ef3553996e29}{p} = 2 * l - q;

    \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} [
        Math.round( \hyperlink{jquery-ui_8js_ad69159066a3e2587e93a13ca2189a482}{hue2rgb}( \hyperlink{media_2js_2jquery_8js_a32d2366ed9853870f0c2ef3553996e29}{p}, q, h + ( 1 / 3 ) ) * 255 ),
        Math.round( \hyperlink{jquery-ui_8js_ad69159066a3e2587e93a13ca2189a482}{hue2rgb}( \hyperlink{media_2js_2jquery_8js_a32d2366ed9853870f0c2ef3553996e29}{p}, q, h ) * 255 ),
        Math.round( \hyperlink{jquery-ui_8js_ad69159066a3e2587e93a13ca2189a482}{hue2rgb}( \hyperlink{media_2js_2jquery_8js_a32d2366ed9853870f0c2ef3553996e29}{p}, q, h - ( 1 / 3 ) ) * 255 ),
        \hyperlink{chosen_8jquery_8min_8js_a4124bc0a9335c27f086f24ba207a4912}{a}
    ];
\}
\end{DoxyCode}
